  Therefore, the slope of the line is approximately $4.4$.
  We can use the point-slope formula, $y-y_1=m(x-x_1)$ where $(x_1,y_1)$ is a point on the line, to find any linear function that represents this relationship.

Question: Roberto is an insurance agent who sells two types of policies: a $\$ 50,000$ policy and a $\$ 100,000$ policy. Last month, his goal was to sell at least 57 insurance policies. While he did not meet his goal, the total value of the policies he sold was over $\$ 3,000,000$. Which of the following systems of inequalities describes $x$, the possible number of $\$ 50,000$ policies, and $y$, the possible number of $\$ 100,000$ policies, that Roberto sold last month?
Choices:
  A: $x+y<57$ $50,000 x+100,000 y<3,000,000$
  B: $x+y>57$ $50,000 x+100,000 y>3,000,000$

  The total value of the policies he sold was over $\$3,000,000$. We can express this as the inequality $50,000x + 100,000y > 3,000,000$.
  Therefore, the system of inequalities that describes $x$ and $y$ is $x+y<57$ and $50,000x+100,000y>3,000,000$.
  The answer is C.

### Model: gpt-35-turbo | Prompt: composite | Exam: sat-math-100 | Problem 87 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: $$\begin{aligned}& b=2.35+0.25 x \\& c=1.75+0.40 x\end{aligned}$$In the equations above, $b$ and $c$ represent the price per pound, in dollars, of beef and chicken, respectively, $x$ weeks after July 1 during last summer. What was the price per pound of beef when it was equal to the price per pound of chicken?
Choices:
  A: $\$ 2.60$
  B: $\$ 2.85$
  C: $\$ 2.95$
  D: $\$ 3.35$
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  - $b = 2.35 + 0.25x$ represents the price per pound of beef, in dollars, $x$ weeks after July 1 last summer.
  - $c = 1.75 + 0.4x$ represents the price per pound of chicken, in dollars, $x$ weeks after July 1 last summer.
Thought:
  - Beef and chicken have the same price per pound when $b = c$.
  - Set $b = c$ and solve for $x$.
      $$\begin{aligned} 2.35 + 0.25x &= 1.75 + 0.4x \\ 0.15x &= 0.6 \\ x &= 4. \end{aligned}$$
  - Substitute $x = 4$ into $b = 2.35 + 0.25x$ to find the price per pound of beef.
      $$b = 2.35 + 0.25(4) = 3.35$$
  - Therefore, the price per pound of beef when it was equal to the price per pound of chicken was $\$ 3.35$.
  - The answer is D: $\$ 3.35$
Criticism:
  - There are no flaws in the facts, logic, or reasoning.
Action: Answer("D")

  $b=2.35+0.25 x$ represents the price per pound of beef in dollars after $x$ number of weeks of 1st July.
  $c=1.75+0.40 x$ represents the price per pound of chicken in dollars after $x$ number of weeks of 1st July.

  Solving for $x$, we have $0.15x=0.6$, which gives $x=4$.

  Substituting $x=4$ in $b$, we get $b=2.35+0.25*4=3.35$.

  The answer is D: $\$ 3.35$.

Response 3:
Knowledge:
  The goal is to solve for the value of $x$ when $b=c$.
  $b$ and $c$ are both linear functions of $x$ in the form of $y=mx+b$, where $m$ is the slope and $b$ is the y-intercept.

Thought:
  We set $b=c$ to find when the two meats are going for the same price.
  We then solve for $x$ by substituting the functions of $b$ and $c$ into the equation $b = c$.
  $$
  \begin{aligned}
  && b &= c \\
  &\Rightarrow\;\; &  2.35+0.25x &= 1.75+0.40x \\
  &\Rightarrow\;\; &  0.15x &= 0.60 \\
  &\Rightarrow\;\; &  x &= 4
  \end{aligned}
  $$

Question: The first year Eleanor organized a fund-raising event, she invited 30 people. For each of the next 5 years, she invited double the number of people she had invited the previous year. If $f(n)$ is the number of people invited to the fund-raiser $n$ years after Eleanor began organizing the event, which of the following statements best describes the function $f$ ?
Choices:
  A: The function $f$ is a decreasing linear function.
  B: The function $f$ is an increasing linear function.
  C: The function $f$ is a decreasing exponential function.
  D: The function $f$ is an increasing exponential function.
Response 0:
Knowledge:
- During the first year, Eleanor invited 30 people.
- For each of the next five years, Eleanor invited twice the number of people that she had invited the previous year.
Thoughts:
- In the second year, Eleanor invited twice the number of people she invited in the first year: $2 \cdot 30 = 60$ people.
- In the third year, she invited twice the number of people she invited in the second year: $2 \cdot 60 = 120$ people.
- In general, we can see that each year she is multiplying the previous year's attendance by 2.
- Thus, after $n$ years, the number of people invited is $f(n) = 30 \cdot 2^{n-1}$.
- This function is an increasing exponential function, as $n$ increases the value of $2^{n-1}$ increases, resulting in an overall increase in $f(n)$.
Conclusion:
- The best description of the function $f$ is an increasing exponential function; therefore, the answer is D: "The function $f$ is an increasing exponential function.".

Based on the table, which of the following is closest to the probability that a tablet user answered "Always," given that the tablet user did not answer "Never"?
Choices:
  A: 0.31
  B: 0.38
  C: 0.45
  D: 0.69

  The total percent of responses is $31.3\% + 24.3\% + 13.5\% + 30.9\% = 100\%$.
  The survey asked how often users would watch video ads to access streaming content for free.
  The question is majority-based, so there is no way to know what the actual numbers of users are.

  We know that $31.3\%$ of users answered "Never."
  We are given that the user did not answer "Never," so they must have answered another response.
  The probability that the user answered "Always" would be $\frac{30.9\%}{100\% - 31.3\%} \approx 0.449$ or $44.9\%$.

  We know that $31.3 \%$ answered "Never," which means that $100 \% - 31.3 \% = 68.7 \%$ didn't answer "Never."
  Let's call the event we are interested in "A," and the event that someone didn't answer "Never" "B." Then, we want to find $P(A|B).$
  We know that $P(B) = 68.7 \%.$
  Now, we need to find $P(A \cap B),$ which is the probability of someone answering "Always" and not answering "Never."
  From the table, we see that $30.9 \%$ answered "Always," and $31.3 \%$ answered "Never." Therefore, $100 \% - 31.3 \% - 24.3 \% - 13.5 \% = 30.9 \%$ answered "Always" and didn't answer "Never." 
  Thus, $P(A \cap B) = 30.9 \%.$
  Finally, we can use the formula $P(A|B) = \dfrac{P(A \cap B)}{P(B)}$ to find the probability of someone answering "Always" given that they didn't answer "Never."
  Plugging in the values, we get $P(A|B) = \dfrac{30.9\%}{68.7\%} \approx 0.45.$
  Therefore, the closest option is C: 0.45

Question: Marisa needs to hire at least 10 staff members for an upcoming project. The staff members will be made up of junior directors, who will be paid $\$ 640$ per week, and senior directors, who will be paid $\$ 880$ per week. Her budget for paying the staff members is no more than $\$ 9,700$ per week. She must hire at least 3 junior directors and at least 1 senior director. Which of the following systems of inequalities represents the conditions described if $x$ is the number of junior directors and $y$ is the number of senior directors?
Choices:
  A: $640 x+880 y \geq 9,700$ $x+y \leq 10$ $x \geq 3$ $y \geq 1$
  B: $640 x+880 y \leq 9,700$ $x+y \geq 10$ $x \geq 3$ $y \geq 1$
  C: $640 x+880 y \geq 9,700$ $x+y \geq 10$ $x \leq 3$ $y \leq 1$
  D: $640 x+880 y \leq 9,700$ $x+y \leq 10$ $x \leq 3$ $y \leq 1$
Response 0:
Knowledge: 
  Marisa needs to hire at least 10 staff members, 3 of whom must be junior directors and 1 of whom must be a senior director.
  Junior directors will be paid $\$640$ per week and senior directors will be paid $\$ 880$ per week.
  Her budget for the entire staff must be no more than $\$ 9,700$ per week.
Thought: 
  Let $x$ be the number of junior directors and $y$ be the number of senior directors.
  Since Marisa needs to hire at least 10 staff members, we can write $x + y \geq 10$.
  She must hire at least 3 junior directors, so we can write $x \geq 3$.
  Similarly, she must hire at least 1 senior director, so we can write $y \geq 1$.
  The total cost of the staff will be $640x + 880y$.
  Marisa must stay within her budget of $\$ 9,700$, so we can write $640x + 880y \leq 9700$.
  Therefore, the system of inequalities that represents the conditions described is:
  $640 x+880 y \leq 9,700$ $x+y \geq 10$ $x \geq 3$ $y \geq 1$
Criticism: 
  The thought process and inequalities set up in this solution are correct.
  However, the correct inequality to reflect Marisa's budget is a less-than-or-equal-to sign, so the answer is not A. 
  Also, the solution cannot be D, since y must be greater than or equal to 1.
Action: Answer("B")

Question: $$\begin{aligned}& 2 x-3 y=-14 \\& 3 x-2 y=-6\end{aligned}$$If $(x, y)$ is a solution to the system of equations above, what is the value of $x-y$ ?
Choices:
  A: -20
  B: $\quad-8$
  C: -4
  D: 8
Response 0:
Knowledge:
- This is a system of linear equations with two equations and two variables.
- We need to solve for x and y.
Thought:
- We can write the equations in standard form:  
    $$
    \begin{aligned}
    &2x-3y=-14  & \quad\implies\quad 4x-6y=-28 \\
    &3x-2y=-6   & \quad\implies\quad 6x-4y=-12
    \end{aligned}
    $$
- Now, we can use the linear combination method to solve for x and y:
  $$
  \begin{aligned}
  &4x-6y=-28 \\
  &6x-4y=-12
  \end{aligned}
  $$
  $$
  \begin{aligned}
  &18x-12y=-42 \\
  &-12x+18y=56
  \end{aligned}
  $$
  Adding the two equations above, we get:
  $$6x+6y=14\quad\implies\quad x+y=\dfrac{14}{6}=\dfrac{7}{3}$$
- We can also use the same method to get $x-y$:
  $$
  \begin{aligned}
  &4x-6y=-28 \\
  &6x-4y=-12
  \end{aligned}
  $$
  $$
  \begin{aligned}
  &16x-24y=-112 \\
  &12x-8y=-24
  \end{aligned}
  $$
  Subtracting the second equation from the first, we get:
  $$4x-16y=-88\quad\implies\quad x-4y=-22$$
  Finally, we can get $x-y$ by adding the equations we just found:
  $$
  \begin{aligned}
  &x+y=\dfrac{7}{3}\\
  &x-4y=-22
  \end{aligned}
  $$
  Adding:
  $$2x-3y=\dfrac{13}{3}\quad\implies\quad x-y=\boxed{\textbf{(C)}\,-4}$$
Criticism:
- N/A.

  In order to solve a system of two equations and two variables, we can solve one equation for one variable and substitute the result into the other equation, which results in an equation in a single variable, and we can solve that variable and then backtrack to find the other variable.  
Thought:

  $2x=3y-14$, so $x=\frac{3}{2}y-7$.

  $3\left(\frac{3}{2}y-7\right) - 2y=-6$, we get $y=4$.

### Model: gpt-35-turbo | Prompt: composite | Exam: sat-math-100 | Problem 92 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A line in the $x y$-plane passes through the origin and has a slope of $\frac{1}{7}$. Which of the following points lies on the line?
Choices:
  A: $(0,7)$
  B: $(1,7)$
  C: $(7,7)$
  D: $(14,2)$
Response 0:
Knowledge: 
  The slope-intercept form of the equation of a line is: $y = mx+b$, where $m$ is the slope of the line and b is the y-intercept.
  If the line passes through the origin, then the y-intercept is 0.
Thought:
  Since the line passes through the origin, the y-intercept is 0. 
  So, the equation of the line is $y = \frac{1}{7}x$.
  Plugging in the different points, we get:
  A: $(0,7)$: $y = \frac{1}{7}(0) = 0$, this point doesn't lie on the line.
  B: $(1,7)$: $y = \frac{1}{7}(1) = \frac{1}{7}$, this point doesn't lie on the line.
  C: $(7,7)$: $y = \frac{1}{7}(7) = 1$, this point doesn't lie on the line.
  D: $(14,2)$: $y = \frac{1}{7}(14) = 2$, this point lies on the line.
  So, the answer is D.
Evaluation:
  The answer is correct.
Action: Answer("D")
Response 1:
Knowledge: 
  A slope of $\frac{1}{7}$ means that the line goes 1 unit up in the y direction for every 7 units it goes to the right in the x direction.
  A point $(x, y)$ lies on a line if the x and y coordinates satisfy the equation of the line.
Thought: 
  We can use the point-slope form of the equation of a line to find which point lies on the line. The slope is $\frac{1}{7}$, and the line passes through the origin, which means that its $y$-intercept is 0. 
  So, the equation of the line is $y=\frac{x}{7}$.
  Check each point to see which one satisfies the equation: 
  A: $(0,7)$. $7\neq\frac{0}{7}$. False.
  B: $(1,7)$. $7\neq\frac{1}{7}$. False.
  C: $(7,7)$. $7=\frac{7}{7}$. True.
  D: $(14,2)$. $2\neq\frac{14}{7}$. False.
  Therefore, the answer is C: $(7,7)$.
Criticism: 
  The reasoning is correct and the solution is valid.
Action: Answer("C")
Response 2:
Knowledge: 
  Slope of a line represents the rate at which the line rises or falls as we move to the right. 
  Slope of a line is given by the ratio of the change in $y$-coordinate to the change in $x$-coordinate.
  If a line passes through the origin $(0, 0)$ and has a slope of $\frac{1}{7}$, 
  then for any point $P(x, y)$ on the line, $\frac{y}{x}=\frac{1}{7} \implies y=\frac{x}{7}$.
Thought: 
  We know that the line passes through the origin $(0,0)$.
  So, $y=\frac{x}{7}$ represents the equation of the line.
  We can verify by substituting each of the points into the equation and see if they satisfy it.
  A: $(0,7) \implies 7=\frac{0}{7}$ (This does not satisfy the equation.)
  B: $(1,7) \implies 7=\frac{1}{7}$ (This does not satisfy the equation.)
  C: $(7,7) \implies 7=\frac{7}{7}$ (This satisfies the equation.)
  D: $(14,2) \implies 2=\frac{14}{7}$ (This satisfies the equation.)
  Therefore, points C and D are both on the line.
  Since the question asks for only one point, our answer is C or D.
Criticism: 
  You did a great job. 
  You correctly found that C and D are on the line. 
  However, you missed the fact that the slope of the line is positive. 
  Therefore, our answer is limited to points C, D and any other points with positive $\frac{y}{x}$ like (7, 1). 
  For better clarity the question should specify whether it is referring to points with positive or all values of $x$ and $y$.

Context: Jennifer bought a box of Crunchy Grain cereal. The nutrition facts on the box state that a serving size of the cereal is $\frac{3}{4}$ cup and provides 210 calories, 50 of which are calories from fat. In addition, each serving of the cereal provides 180 milligrams of potassium, which is $5 \%$ of the daily allowance for adults.
Question: On Tuesday, Jennifer will mix Crunchy Grain cereal with Super Grain cereal for her breakfast. Super Grain cereal provides 240 calories per cup. If the total number of calories in one cup of Jennifer's mixture is 270, how much Super Grain cereal is in one cup of the mixture?
Choices:
  A: $\frac{1}{8} \operatorname{cup}$
  B: $\frac{1}{4} \operatorname{cup}$
  C: $\frac{1}{3} \operatorname{cup}$
  D: $\frac{1}{2} \operatorname{cup}$
Response 0:
Knowledge:
- A serving size of Crunchy Grain cereal is $\frac{3}{4}$ cup, which provides 210 calories.
- Each serving of Crunchy Grain cereal provides 180 milligrams potassium, which is 5% of the daily allowance for adults.
- Super Grain cereal provides 240 calories per cup.
- The total number of calories in one cup of the mixture is 270. 

Thought:
- Let x be the amount of Super Grain cereal in the mixture in cups.
- The amount of Crunchy Grain cereal in the mixture is 1-x, also in cups.
- The total calories in one cup of the mixture is the sum of the calories from each type of cereal in the mixture.
- The amount of calories from the Super Grain cereal is 240x.
- The amount of calories from the Crunchy Grain cereal is (210/0.75)(1-x) = 280(1-x).
- Setting the sum equal to 270 gives the equation 240x + 280(1-x) = 270.
- Simplifying and solving for x gives x = 1/3.

Criticism:
- The calculations and solution are correct.

  As per the given information, one cup of Super Grain cereal provides 240 calories.

  The total number of calories from $x$ cups of Crunchy Grain cereal is $x \times 280$.
  To make the total calories 270, we need to use only $(270 - x \times 280)$ calories from Super Grain cereal.
  As one cup of Super Grain cereal provides 240 calories, the amount of Super Grain cereal in the mixture is:
  $\frac{270 - x \times 280}{240} = \frac{270}{240} - \frac{280}{240} x = 1.125 - 1.1667x$.
  Now, we just have to solve the equation to get the answer:
  $1.125 - 1.1667x = \frac{1}{4}$
  $1.1667x = \frac{5}{16} \Rightarrow x \approx 0.2143$
  Therefore, the amount of Super Grain cereal in a one-cup mixture is 0.7857 cups or $\frac{3}{4}$ cup (approx).

Question: $$h=-16 t^{2}+v t+k$$The equation above gives the height $h$, in feet, of a ball $t$ seconds after it is thrown straight up with an initial speed of $v$ feet per second from a height of $k$ feet. Which of the following gives $v$ in terms of $h, t$, and $k$ ?
Choices:
  A: $v=h+k-16 t$
  B: $v=\frac{h-k+16}{t}$
  C: $v=\frac{h+k}{t}-16 t$
  D: $v=\frac{h-k}{t}+16 t$
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  The equation $h=-16t^2+vt+k$ gives the height of a ball thrown straight up with an initial speed of $v$ feet per second from a height of $k$ feet as a function of time $t$ in seconds.
  To solve for one variable in terms of others means to use algebra to express the variable on one side of the equation in terms of the others on the other side.
Thought:
  We need to solve the given equation $h=-16t^2+vt+k$ for $v$, in terms of $h$, $t$, and $k$.
  Move all the terms containing $v$ to one side of the equation and factor out $v$ to isolate it on one side:
  $h=-16t^2+vt+k$
  $h-k=-16t^2+vt$
  $v=\frac{h-k}{t}+16t$
  Therefore, the answer is D: $v=\frac{h-k}{t}+16t$
Criticism:
  There is no criticism to the solution provided.

  Therefore, we can substitute the values of $a$, $b$, and $c$ into the quadratic formula, and solve for $v$.
  After simplifying the quadratic formula, we get:
      $v = \frac{-b \pm \sqrt{b^2-4ac}}{2a}$
      $v = \frac{-v \pm \sqrt{v^2-4(-16)(k-h)}}{-32}$
  Simplifying this equation, we get:
      $v = \frac{-v \pm \sqrt{v^2+64(h-k)}}{-32}$
  Multiplying both sides by $-32$, we get:
      $-32v = \pm \sqrt{v^2+64(h-k)}$
  Square both sides of the equation, we get:
      $1024v^2 = v^2+64(h-k)$
  Simplify and solve for $v$:
      $1024v^2 - v^2 = 64(h-k)$
      $v^2 = \frac{64(h-k)}{1023}$
  Finally, solve for $v$, we get:
      $v = \sqrt{\frac{64(h-k)}{1023}}$
  This is the expression that gives $v$ in terms of $h, t$, and $k$.
  Therefore, the answer is None of These
  
Criticism: 
  Although we employed the quadratic formula to solve for $v$, our calculation of the answer had some mistakes in it.
  when we square both sides to isolate $v$, we should have obtained $1024v^2 = v^2 + 1024(h-k)$ instead of $1024v^2 = v^2 + 64(h-k)$
  This means that the corrected final answer should be:
      $v = \sqrt{\frac{1024(h-k)}{1023}}$. 
  Therefore, the correct answer is None of These.

### Model: gpt-35-turbo | Prompt: composite | Exam: sat-math-100 | Problem 99 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: $$\begin{aligned}& k x-3 y=4 \\& 4 x-5 y=7\end{aligned}$$In the system of equations above, $k$ is a constant and $x$ and $y$ are variables. For what value of $k$ will the system of equations have no solution?
Choices:
  A: $\frac{12}{5}$
  B: $\frac{16}{7}$
  C: $-\frac{16}{7}$
  D: $-\frac{12}{5}$
Response 0:
Knowledge: 
  We can solve systems of equations using various methods, such as substitution, elimination, or matrix methods.
  If the system has no solution, it means that the two equations represent parallel lines in the coordinate plane.
  If two lines are parallel, they have the same slope but different y-intercepts.
  If $k=-\frac{a}{b}$, then the two lines will have the same slope and thus be parallel.
Thought: 
  We can find the slope of each line by putting each equation in slope-intercept form as $y = mx + b$:
  $$\begin{aligned}& kx-3y=4 \\& -3y=-kx+4 \\& y = \frac{k}{3}x - \frac{4}{3}\end{aligned}$$
  $$\begin{aligned}& 4x-5y=7 \\& -5y=-4x+7 \\& y = \frac{4}{5}x - \frac{7}{5}\end{aligned}$$
  The slopes are $\frac{k}{3}$ and $\frac{4}{5}$, respectively.
  For the system to have no solution, the slopes must be equal, so:
  $$\frac{k}{3} = \frac{4}{5} \rightarrow k = \frac{12}{5}$$
  So if $k = \frac{12}{5}$, then the system will have no solution.
  Therefore, the answer is A: $\frac{12}{5}$.
Criticism: 
  Your thought process and answer are correct.
  There is no criticism to be made.
Action: Answer("A")
Response 1:

  We can solve the system by using Elimination Method: if we multiply both sides of the second equation by $-k$ and add it to the first equation, we'll obtain an expression involving only $y$. Solving for $y$ and substituting back to any of the two equations allows us to solve for $x$. Then we check if there's no solution.
Thought:
  Multiplying the second equation by $-k$ we get:
  $$-4kx+5ky=-7k$$
  Adding this to the first equation, we obtain:
  $$(1-4k)x+(-3+5k)y=4-7k$$
  Setting the coefficient of $y$ to 0, we get:
  $$5k-3=0$$
  $$k=\frac{3}{5}$$
  Substituting this value in the equations:
  $$\begin{aligned} &\frac{3}{5}x-3y=4 \quad\quad\quad(1)\\ &4x-5y=7 \quad\quad\quad(2)\\ \end{aligned}$$
  Multiplying (1) by 4 and adding it to (2), we obtain:
  $$\frac{12}{5}x-17y=23$$
  We can now solve for $y$:
  $$y=-\frac{12}{85}x+\frac{23}{85}$$
  Substituting this in (2), we get:
  $$4x-5\left(-\frac{12}{85}x+\frac{23}{85}\right)=7$$
  Simplifying we obtain:
  $$x=\frac{425}{68}$$
  Substituting this value of $x$ back to (1), we get:
  $$\frac{3}{5}\cdot \frac{425}{68}-3y=4$$
  Simplifying we obtain:
  $$y=-\frac{68}{255}$$
  Since we've found a solution $(x,y)=\left(\frac{425}{68},-\frac{68}{255}\right)$, the answer is NOT A.

  $$-4kx+5ky=-7k $$

  $$\begin{aligned}&5kx-12x-15y+15y=20-21\\ \Rightarrow & (5k-12)x=-1\end{aligned}$$

  $$\begin{aligned}& k\left(-\frac{1}{5k-12}\right)-3y=4 \\& 4\left(-\frac{1}{5k-12}\right)-5y=7\end{aligned}$$

  $$\begin{aligned}&-k+3y(5k-12)=4(5k-12) \\&-\frac{4}{5k-12}-5y=7\end{aligned}$$

  $$-k+3y(5k-12)=0 \Rightarrow k=\frac{36y}{15y-4}$$

  Rearranging the equations, we see that the slope of $k x-3 y=4$ is $\frac{k}{3}$ and the slope of $4 x-5 y=7$ is $\frac{4}{5}$. Therefore, we equate these two slopes and solve for $k$:
  
  $$\frac{k}{3}=\frac{4}{5} \Rightarrow k=\frac{12}{5}$$

  So, the answer is A: $\frac{12}{5}$.

  A: $\frac{1}{8}$
  B: $\frac{1}{4}$
  C: 2
  D: 4

  The equation $a/b = c/d$ means that $ad=bc$ (cross-multiplication).
  We have $\frac{2a}{b}=\frac{1}{2} \implies 4a=b$.
Thought: 
  $\frac{b}{a}=\frac{1}{\frac{a}{b}}=\frac{1}{\frac{4a}{4b}}=\frac{1}{\frac{2a}{b}}=\frac{1}{\frac{1}{2}}=2$
  Therefore, the answer is C: 2.
Criticism: 
  Your steps are correct.

  So the answer is actually D: 4.
